## Analysis

The Ground Truth (GT) is:
$$-0.4466 \cdot A \cdot \exp(-0.08660 \cdot t) + 0.9910 \cdot \sin(\sqrt{A})$$

I need to find candidates that can match this structure: a term proportional to $A \cdot \exp(\text{const} \cdot t)$ plus a term involving $\sin(\sqrt{A})$.

Note that $\sin(\sqrt{A}) = \cos(\sqrt{A} - \pi/2)$, so any candidate with $\cos(\sqrt{A} \cdot c_4 + c_5)$ can represent $\sin(\sqrt{A})$ by setting $c_4 = 1$ and $c_5 = -\pi/2$.
